#+TITLE: CAG Refactor Plan — Eliminating Axioms / Parameters / Conjectures
#+DATE: 2026-05-01
#+AUTHOR: Orchestrator + α/β/γ rotating subagents

* Overview

Worker-pool rotation: 3 subagents (α, β, γ) plus me as orchestrator (4 total
per box budget). Each subagent grabs the next available task from the queue
when their current task finishes. Single-file `coqc` for verification (never
`make` simultaneously, so rocq is always free for someone to compile-check).

Key invariant: when a task ships its result, dependent tasks become unblocked.
The orchestrator (me) routes the next-available agent to the highest-ROI
unblocked task.

* Status legend
- [ ] queued (waiting)
- [-] in progress (assigned to an agent)
- [X] complete

* Worker-pool schema

#+BEGIN_EXAMPLE
                Round 1 (no cross-agent deps)
   ┌──────────────┐  ┌─────────────────┐  ┌─────────────────┐
   │ α: Task M.0  │  │ β: Task F       │  │ γ: Task V       │
   │ Mat_wf found │  │ FIS strengthen  │  │ Vm_mod Def      │
   └──────┬───────┘  └────────┬────────┘  └────────┬────────┘
          │                   │                    │
          ▼ done              ▼ done               ▼ done
   ┌──────────────┐  ┌─────────────────┐  ┌─────────────────┐
   │ α: Task A    │  │ β: Task M.1     │  │ γ: Task M.2     │
   │ AxClMor set. │  │ SpecLin+Orth    │  │ Symplec+LieAlg  │
   └──────┬───────┘  └────────┬────────┘  └────────┬────────┘
          │                   │                    │
          ▼ done              ▼ done               ▼ done
                  ... (continue rotation through queue)
#+END_EXAMPLE

* Independent tasks (no cross-agent deps; can launch any time)

** TODO Task M.0 — Mat_wf foundation [Agent α, Round 1]
SCOPE: =theories/Lie/Linear.v=
- [ ] Add =Mat_wf n n A= hypothesis to ~12 base matrix axioms
- [ ] Restructure =gl_vs= to take an =n= parameter
- [ ] Set =gl_vs.(vsF_zero) := mat_zero fld n=
- [ ] Update internal proof terms (=vsF_add_zero_r=, =vsF_add_neg_r=, etc.)
CONTRACT (signatures the consumers depend on):
#+BEGIN_SRC coq
Axiom mat_add_zero_r_wf : forall {F} (fld : Field F) (n : nat) (A : Matrix F),
    Mat_wf n n A -> mat_add fld A (mat_zero fld n) = A.
Axiom mat_add_neg_wf : forall {F} (fld : Field F) (n : nat) (A : Matrix F),
    Mat_wf n n A -> mat_add fld A (mat_neg fld A) = mat_zero fld n.
Axiom mat_mul_assoc_m_wf : forall {F} (fld : Field F) (n : nat) (A B C : Matrix F),
    Mat_wf n n A -> Mat_wf n n B -> Mat_wf n n C ->
    mat_mul fld (mat_mul fld A B n) C n = mat_mul fld A (mat_mul fld B C n) n.
(* ... etc. *)
Definition gl_vs {F} (fld : Field F) (n : nat) : VectorSpaceF fld { A : Matrix F | Mat_wf n n A } := ...
#+END_SRC
UNLOCKS: Tasks M.1, M.2 (~25 axioms total)

       * New helper Definitions =sum_seq= / =sum_seq_aux= (right-associated finite sum).
       * New axiom-free Local Lemmas: =sum_seq_aux_ext=, =sum_seq_ext=,
         =sum_seq_aux_zero=, =sum_seq_zero=, =sum_seq_aux_add=, =sum_seq_add=,
         =sum_seq_aux_shift=, =sum_seq_S=, =sum_seq_swap= (Fubini),

         =fold_left_dot_as_sum_seq=, =mat_mul_entry_sum=,
         =mat_mul_diag_sum=, =mat_trace_mul_double_sum=.
       * Final =mat_trace_cyclic= proof: convert both sides to the
         double sum [Σ_i Σ_j _[i,j] · _[j,i]], swap via Fubini, then
         apply =cr_mul_comm= pointwise.
- [X] =Print Assumptions mat_trace_cyclic= = "Closed under the global
       context" (zero axiom dependencies — the proof works directly
       at the [fold_left] level and bypasses [mat_mul_assoc_m] /
       [mat_mul_add_distr_*]). Same for =mat_trace_bracket_zero=.
- [-] Secondary: =gl_sl_sub_derived=. Surveyed and left as
       paper-attributed Axiom (Humphreys §1.2). Diagnosis added in
       a multi-line in-source comment: requires (1) canonical
       decomposition  A = Σ A[i,j]·e_{ij}  for any [Mat_wf n n A]
       at the list-of-lists level + (2) sum-induction for subalgebra
       membership. Both are multi-day spanning-infra tasks (analogous
       to Task DG-style structural lifts) — beyond M.1.next scope.
DELIVERED: −1 axiom (=mat_trace_cyclic= Axiom → Lemma);
13+ new axiom-free Local helpers in SpecialLinear.v.

*** DONE Task M.2.next.followup.2 — discharge AG.v mmul axioms [Agent β, Round 7 — 2026-05-01]
DEPENDS: Task M.2.next.followup
SCOPE: =theories/AG.v= only (no other files modified)
The three foundational matrix-multiplication axioms in =AG.v= were
preventing fully-axiom-free compilation of all CComplex matrix-side
results.  This round ports the [sum_seq] / Fubini infrastructure
into AG.v itself (so AG.v's downstream consumers Representation.v,
Character.v can use the sound forms) and discharges the three axioms
to =_wf= Lemma counterparts.

       397–626): =sum_seq_aux=, =sum_seq=, =sum_seq_aux_ext=,

       =sum_seq_distr_l=, =sum_seq_aux_distr_r=, =sum_seq_distr_r=

       =nth_default_app_sing_lt/_eq=, =nth_default_row_mul_mcols=,
       =nth_mmul_row=, =nth_default_map_col=,

       =A : n×p=, =B : p×q=).

       =row_ext_nth_default=, =mat_ext_wf= (Mat_wf-guarded

       =mident_nth=, =nth_default_mident=.
- [X] New Kronecker-collapse Lemmas: =sum_seq_kron_l=, =sum_seq_kron_r=
       (Σ over [if k =? j then C1 else C0] · f j collapses to f k).
- [X] **Lemma =mmul_mident_right_wf=** (=AG.v:907=):
       =Mat_wf n n A -> mmul A (mident n) n = A=.  Discharged via
       =mat_mul_entry_sum= + =sum_seq_kron_r=.
- [X] **Lemma =mmul_mident_left_wf=** (=AG.v:925=):
       =Mat_wf n n A -> mmul (mident n) A n = A=.  Discharged via
       =mat_mul_entry_sum= + =sum_seq_kron_l=.
- [X] **Lemma =mmul_assoc_wf=** (=AG.v:946=):
       =Mat_wf n m A -> Mat_wf m p B -> Mat_wf p q C ->
       mmul A (mmul B C q) q = mmul (mmul A B p) C q=.
       Discharged via =mat_mul_entry_sum_gen= (×4) +
       =sum_seq_distr_l/_r= + =sum_seq_swap= (Fubini) +
       =AG_Cmul_assoc=.

Bare AXIOMS retained as paper-attributable companions (same
=_wf=-counterpart pattern β R5 used for =mat_vs_add_zero_r=):
- =Axiom mmul_assoc= (un-hypothesised, FALSE-as-stated for
  shape-mismatched matrices: both sides truncate via mmul's =r::rs=
  structure but only one side's truncation matches the other's).
- =Axiom mmul_mident_right= / =mmul_mident_left= (already
  Mat_wf-guarded; trivially follow from the new =_wf= Lemmas, but
  the pattern of leaving the Axiom as a public-API constant is kept
  to minimise Representation.v / Character.v churn — those sites
  already pass Mat_wf hypotheses, so a follow-up trivially swaps the
  =Axiom= references for the =_wf= Lemma references).

*** DONE LieAlgebra residuals [β R8 — 2026-05-01]
DEPENDS: Task M.2.next.followup.2 (β R7's =mmul_assoc_wf=)
SCOPE: =theories/LieAlgebra.v= only (no other files modified)
Discharge of the residual =gl_jacobi_wf= Axiom, lifting the M.2.next
deferral now that =mmul_assoc_wf= is a Lemma.

- [X] **Lemma =gl_jacobi_wf=** (=LieAlgebra.v:1290=, was Axiom @1120):
      =Mat_wf n n A -> Mat_wf n n B -> Mat_wf n n C ->
       madd (madd ([A,[B,C]]) ([B,[C,A]])) ([C,[A,B]]) = mzero n=.
      Proof structure ports =Lie/Linear.v='s =mat_bracket_jacobi= to
      the CComplex / =msub=-bracket setting:
      (1) expand each [X,[Y,Z]] using =mmul_msub_l/_r= (relocated up
          from the killing-form section so they're in scope here);
      (2) apply =mmul_assoc_wf= (β R7) to put each triple in the
          left-associated form T(X,Y,Z) := mmul (mmul X Y n) Z n;
      (3) the 12 signed terms cancel pairwise via 11 association /
          commutation moves + 6 invocations of =mat_vs_add_neg_l/r_wf=,
          following the abstract-Field rewrite sequence in Linear.v
          adjusted for the OPPOSITE direction of =mat_vs_add_assoc=.
- [X] New Local helpers added to support the proof:
      - =mneg_mneg= (involution, =mneg (mneg X) = X=);
      - =mneg_msub= (=−(X−Y) = Y−X=);
      - =mat_vs_add_neg_l_wf= (=−A + A = mzero=);
      - =mat_vs_add_zero_l_wf= (=mzero + A = A=).
      All four axiom-free except the already-cited =CRealEq_eq=.
- [X] Relocated Local Lemmas =mmul_msub_l= and =mmul_msub_r= up
      from the killing-form section (lines ~1846/1878) to just
      before =gl_jacobi_wf= so they're in scope.  =killing_invariant_wf=
      consumers unchanged (the relocation is purely textual).

=Print Assumptions gl_jacobi_wf= → only =Complex.CRealEq_eq= (the
standard CReal→Leibniz bridge).  No =mmul_assoc=, no
=mat_vs_add_zero_r=, no =mat_vs_add_neg_r= — fully discharged.

- [X] **=gl_adjoint_hom=** (=LieAlgebra.v:1582=) — AUDIT, kept as Axiom:
      The statement, after unfolding =gl_adjoint n X Y = gl_bracket n X Y=,
      reads =[[A,B], C] = [[A,C], [B,C]]=.  This is NOT a Lie-algebra
      identity and is FALSE in general.  Concrete 2×2 counterexample
      committed inline:
        A = [[0,1],[0,0]], B = [[0,0],[1,0]], C = [[1,0],[0,-1]].
        Then [A,B] = C ⇒ LHS = [C,C] = 0.
        But [A,C] = -2A, [B,C] = 2B ⇒ RHS = [-2A,2B] = -4[A,B] = -4C ≠ 0.
      The mathematically correct adjoint-hom identity is the
      Jacobi/Leibniz form
          ad([A,B])(C) = ad(A)(ad(B)(C)) - ad(B)(ad(A)(C))
      i.e. =[[A,B], C] = [A,[B,C]] - [B,[A,C]]=, which =adjoint_bracket=
      already proves abstractly for any =LieAlgebra L=.  The current
      Axiom has NO consumers (verified by =grep -r gl_adjoint_hom
      theories/=) so leaving it in place is safe per the "never strip
      non-equivalent theorems" rule.  A future round should REPLACE
      (not discharge) it with the corrected Leibniz-form statement,
      which is then a corollary of =adjoint_bracket= specialised to
      =gl n=.

DELIVERED: **−1 axiom** (=gl_jacobi_wf= Axiom → Lemma), full audit
note + counterexample for =gl_adjoint_hom= (kept-as-Axiom, no consumers).

Compile evidence:
- =rocq compile -Q theories CAG theories/LieAlgebra.v= exits 0.
- =rocq compile -Q theories CAG theories/Lie/Linear.v= exits 0
  (Mat_wf surface intact, =mat_bracket_jacobi= lemma unchanged).
- =rocq compile -Q theories CAG theories/Lie/{BasicDef,Ideals,Homomorphisms,
  Solvable,Nilpotent,Engel,SpecialLinear,Derivations,Radical,Semisimple,
  KillingForm,StructureConstants,LowDimensional,Triangular,Symplectic,
  Orthogonal}.v= all exit 0.

*** DONE Replace false =gl_adjoint_hom= with Leibniz rule [β R9 — 2026-05-01]
DEPENDS: β R8 (=gl_jacobi_wf= Lemma + =mneg_msub= helper)
SCOPE: =theories/LieAlgebra.v= only
Replacement of the false-as-stated =Axiom gl_adjoint_hom= (β R8 audit
with 2×2 counterexample, zero consumers) by the mathematically
correct Leibniz rule for the adjoint, proved as a Lemma.

- [X] DELETED =Axiom gl_adjoint_hom= (=LieAlgebra.v:1604=).  β R8's
      counterexample (2×2 matrices A=[[0,1],[0,0]], B=[[0,0],[1,0]],
      C=[[1,0],[0,-1]] with [A,B]=C) is preserved verbatim as a
      doc comment block on the new Lemma's preceding section.
- [X] NEW **Lemma =gl_leibniz_rule_wf=** (=LieAlgebra.v=, replaces
      the deleted axiom):
      =Mat_wf n n A -> Mat_wf n n B -> Mat_wf n n C ->
       gl_bracket n (gl_bracket n A B) C =
       msub (gl_bracket n A (gl_bracket n B C))
            (gl_bracket n B (gl_bracket n A C))=
      i.e. [[A,B], C] = [A,[B,C]] − [B,[A,C]] (Jacobi rearranged).
      Proof: rearrange =gl_jacobi_wf=
        [A,[B,C]] + [B,[C,A]] + [C,[A,B]] = 0
      using the bracket-swap antisymmetry ([X,Y] = mneg [Y,X], from
      =mneg_msub= via the new local =gl_bracket_swap_neg=) and the
      bracket-second-arg-negation lemma ([B,−X] = mneg [B,X], from
      the new local =gl_bracket_neg_r_local=).
- [X] NEW Local helpers added (all axiom-free except =CRealEq_eq=):
      - =mmul_mneg_l= (=(−Y)·Z = −(Y·Z)=) — factored out of the
        inline proof inside =mmul_msub_l=.
      - =mmul_mneg_r= (=X·(−Z) = −(X·Z)=) — factored out of the
        inline proof inside =mmul_msub_r=.
      - =gl_bracket_swap_neg= ([X,Y] = mneg [Y,X]) — direct from
        =mneg_msub=.
      - =gl_bracket_neg_r_local= ([B,−X] = mneg [B,X]) — uses the
        two new =mmul_mneg_l/r= helpers.

=Print Assumptions gl_leibniz_rule_wf= → only =Complex.CRealEq_eq=.
No =gl_adjoint_hom= (gone), no other axioms.

DELIVERED: **−1 unsound axiom** (=gl_adjoint_hom= deleted), **+1 sound
Lemma** (=gl_leibniz_rule_wf=).  The historical false statement is
preserved in the comment block as documented mathematical history,
not as an active assumption.

* Research-level (out of scope — needs human mathematicians)

The 440 =Conjecture=-labeled entries (Hall, Sylow consequences, Lawton-
Louder-McReynolds, Bass-Lubotzky, Fricke/Horowitz, Kodaira vanishing, hard
Lefschetz, etc.) are open research problems. Coq agents cannot solve them.

* Rotation queue (orchestrator drives this)

When a slot opens, pick from this priority list:
1. Highest ROI unblocked task
2. Prefer tasks whose blast radius is smaller (single-file > multi-file)
3. Prefer tasks whose contract is fully spec'd

Initial queue order (high to low ROI):
1. M.0 → α
2. F → β
3. V → γ
4. A (after M.0 frees α)
5. M.1 (after M.0 → β when β finishes F)
6. M.2 (after M.0 → γ when γ finishes V)
7. C
8. L
9. Z
10. D
11-13. DG, LM, SP (long-haul)

      inductive in Syntax.v (lines ~511-528).  The actual gap was that

      [lift_alg_term] only produces [ax_var] and [ax_app_fn]).

      GeneratedFunctionalTheory.v (lines ~36-69) — the actual lift/subst
      commutation needed for the [theq_ax] case.  Stated as
      =lift_alg_term (subst_term sub t) =
       ax_subst (map lift_alg_term sub) (lift_alg_term t)= under the
      typing premise that [sub] is well-typed [Γ → Γ'].  Mechanical
      induction on the [HasType] derivation via [fix].  REAL Lemma,
      not Axiom.
      NOTE: the form originally specified in this plan
      =ax_lift n (ax_subst sub M) = ax_subst (map (ax_lift n) sub) (ax_lift (S n) M)=
      is FALSE in general (counter-example: [n=0], [sub=[]],
      [M=ax_var 0]: LHS evaluates to [ax_var 1] but RHS to [ax_var 0]).
      The actually usable commutation is the typed [lift_alg_term] form
      above.

      Lemma).  Proof: ~80 lines using a custom strong induction

      bridging in the [theq_cong] case.  =Print Assumptions= shows
      "Closed under the global context" (no axioms whatsoever — not
      even [ax_subst_cong] or [ax_subst_comp]).

that the =cc_phi_hol= placeholder forces =chart_partial_z= to collapse
to =C0= (mirroring =Forms_pq= / =L2_inner=) was checked and found
incorrect.  =cc_phi_hol= is a *field of the chart record*, not a
trivialisation of =cc_phi= / =cc_psi= or of pulled-back functions.
=chart_partial_z M c f p j L= unfolds to a real epsilon-delta
=Rderiv_at= obligation on four partials of =fun z => f (cc_psi c z)=
at point =cc_phi c p=, with arbitrary =f=.  =chart_partial_z_invariance=
therefore demands a real chain-rule witness (Jacobian of the transition
map), not a placeholder.  Documented inline in =Manifold.v= and left
as Conjecture per Conjecture-priority memory.  Real DG.1.5 work
(strengthen =cc_phi_hol=, then prove a real chain rule) remains open.

*** DONE Bundled-Record refactor — HilbertForms [γ R26-redo, 2026-05-01]

      =Parameter HilbertForms : ... -> ... -> HilbertSpace=.
      Now [HilbertForms E p q : HilbertSpace] — the carrier
      [hs_carrier (HilbertForms E p q)], the inner product
      [hs_inner (HilbertForms E p q) : ... -> ... -> CComplex],
      and ALL twelve [HilbertSpace] field axioms (sesquilinearity,
      conjugate-symmetry, positivity, vector-space laws) come for
      free with this declaration as field projections.  They cannot
      drift, be omitted, or fail to apply.

      The bundled [hs_inner (HilbertForms E p q)] (CComplex-valued)
      is now the project's inner product on this space.  Zero
      non-busywork call sites needed updating (the only use was in
      [T_operator_self_adjoint], updated below).

      [hs_carrier (HilbertForms E p q)] (the bundled carrier),
      not the bare [HilbertForms E p q]-as-Type.
- [X] =T_operator= signature updated to
      [hs_carrier (HilbertForms E p q) -> hs_carrier (HilbertForms E p q)].
- [X] =T_operator_self_adjoint= REVERTED from γ R10's trivial-collapse
      [Theorem … admit. Admitted.] to a [Conjecture] with informal-
      definition comment.  γ R10 had the equality holding by
      [reflexivity] under [hilbert_inner := 0%CReal] (vacuous).  Now

*** DONE Bundled-Record refactor — L2_inner [γ R27, 2026-05-01]
SCOPE: =theories/Harmonic/Sobolev.v= primarily; comment-only updates
in =Laplacian.v= / =Weitzenbock.v= / =GreenOperator.v=.
PER directive [feedback_bundled_records.md] (2026-05-01).

STEP 1 — DECISION (option (b)).  Grep evidence:
- =L2_inner= takes [Forms_pq E p q] arguments (smooth pre-completion),
  returns [CReal] (real-projected).
- =hs_inner (HilbertForms E p q)= takes [hs_carrier (HilbertForms E p
  q)] arguments (L² Hilbert completion), returns [CComplex].
- Different signatures, different domains: not the same content.
  Option (a) (delete L2_inner, route through hs_inner) requires
  rewriting [Forms_pq]-typed call sites in 4 downstream files
  ([Laplacian.v] / [Spectral.v] / [Weitzenbock.v] /
  [GreenOperator.v]), exceeding scope.
- Chose option (b): introduce a Record bundling [L2_inner] with its
  5 defining laws, declare the unique instance as a [Parameter],
  retain [L2_inner] as a thin [Definition] wrapper.

STEP 2 — REFACTOR.  In =Sobolev.v=:
- New Record =SmoothL2 E p q= with 6 fields:
  =sl2_inner=, =sl2_inner_sym=, =sl2_inner_add_left=,
  =sl2_inner_nonneg=, =sl2_inner_le_zero=, =sl2_inner_zero_left=.
- New =Parameter L2_struct : forall M E p q, SmoothL2 E p q= — the
  SOLE [Parameter] of the L²-pre-Hilbert layer post γ R27.
- =Definition L2_inner φ ψ := sl2_inner (L2_struct E p q) φ ψ=.
- The 5 floating Axioms (=L2_inner_sym=, =L2_inner_add_left=,
  =L2_inner_nonneg=, =L2_inner_le_zero=, =L2_inner_zero_left=)
  REMOVED.  Re-exposed under the same names as one-liner Lemmas
  via field projection (so downstream rewrite-targets unchanged).
- The 2 Conjectures (=L2_inner_pos=, =L2_inner_zero_iff=) kept
  unchanged — well-typed against the new bundled [L2_inner].

STEP 3 — γ R25 DOWNSTREAM AXIOMS.  None of the 7 γ R25 Axioms
([dbar_adjoint], [laplacian_self_adjoint], [rough_laplacian_nonneg],
[rough_laplacian_self_adjoint], [curv_endomorphism_self_adjoint],
[harmonic_proj_self_adjoint], [green_self_adjoint]) follow from any
single [SmoothL2] field projection — each one relates [L2_inner] of
a non-bundled operator output (=dbar=, =dbar_laplacian=,
=rough_laplacian=, =curv_endomorphism=, =harmonic_proj=, =green_op=)
which is OUTSIDE the [SmoothL2] Record interface.  All 7 stay as
Axioms; comments updated to point to the [SmoothL2] / [L2_struct]
interface and explain why discharge requires content beyond a
single field projection.  Trivial-collapse discharge via
[dbar := forms_pq_zero] etc. would qualify under
[feedback_trivial_collapse_busywork.md] and is rejected.

*** DONE Bundled-Record refactor — sobolev_norm via SobolevNorm [γ R28, 2026-05-01]
SCOPE: =theories/Harmonic/Sobolev.v= only.
PER directive [feedback_bundled_records.md] (2026-05-01); follows
the immediate γ R27 [SmoothL2]/[L2_struct] template.

PRIOR STATE (post γ R24).  Bare =Parameter sobolev_norm= surrounded
by 4 floating =Axiom=s in =Sobolev.v=:
- =sobolev_norm_zero_is_L2= (order-0 ↔ L²),
- =sobolev_norm_nonneg=,
- =sobolev_norm_monotone= (cross-[k]),
- =sobolev_norm_zero=.

STEP 1 — DECISION (per-[k] Record + 1 retained floating Axiom).
Picked option (a) of the γ R28 plan.  Three of the four laws fit
within a single per-[k] Record =SobolevNorm M E k=.  The fourth law
[sobolev_norm_monotone] compares values across DIFFERENT [k]s, so it
cannot be a field of a Record indexed by a single [k].  Options (b)
(family-indexed Record) and (c) (forall-quantified cross-[k] field)
were considered and rejected as net-ergonomic-loss bundlings — see
the inline rationale comment in =Sobolev.v=.

STEP 2 — REFACTOR.  In =Sobolev.v=:
- New Record =SobolevNorm M E k= with 4 fields:
  =sn_norm=, =sn_norm_nonneg=, =sn_norm_zero=, =sn_norm_at_zero=.
  The fourth field is the order-0 base-case agreement
  =sn_norm conn φ = sl2_inner (L2_struct E p q) φ φ= guarded by
  =k = 0=, threading the γ R27 [L2_struct] interface through the
  W^{0,2} layer.
- New =Parameter sobolev_struct : forall M E k, SobolevNorm E k= —
  the SOLE [Parameter] of the W^{k,2} layer (post γ R28); its three
  per-[k] defining laws are field projections, not floating Axioms.
- =Definition sobolev_norm conn k φ := sn_norm (sobolev_struct E k) conn φ=.
- The 3 per-[k] floating Axioms (=sobolev_norm_zero_is_L2=,
  =sobolev_norm_nonneg=, =sobolev_norm_zero=) REMOVED.  Re-exposed
  under the same names as one-liner Lemmas via field projection
  (downstream rewrite-target names unchanged).
- =sobolev_norm_monotone= retained as the SOLE floating Axiom of
  the W^{k,2} layer; rationale comment in =Sobolev.v= explains why.

STEP 3 — DOWNSTREAM.  Grep evidence: no consumer of =sobolev_norm=
or its 4 axioms in code.  Only =Garding.v= mentions =sobolev_norm=
in a comment.  Cascading-edit risk = nil.

axioms (Calc/Manifold, Lie/Linear), or in the avoid list.

under the 2-cluster cap rather than picking a low-quality second
target.  The audit value is the inventory itself plus a strong
empirical signal that the directive's anti-pattern is now rare in
the project.

REFACTOR — =LocalSystems.v= (only one in scope needing work):
- The pair =Parameter pi1 : ComplexManifold -> Type= +
  =Parameter pi1_group : forall M, StrictGroup (pi1 M)= was a
  textbook shallow-Type-tag-with-dependent-structure pattern: the
  carrier and its group structure could (in principle) drift apart.
- NEW Record =Pi1Group= bundles =pi1_carrier :> Type= (with coercion)
  + =pi1_strict : StrictGroup pi1_carrier= as a single Record
  (analog of the bundled-Record idiom from the project's good
  abstractions).
- Replaced =Parameter pi1= and =Parameter pi1_group= with a SINGLE
  Parameter =pi1_data : ComplexManifold -> Pi1Group= returning the
  bundled Record.
- Re-exposed =pi1= and =pi1_group= as =Definition= projections
  (=pi1_carrier (pi1_data M)= and =pi1_strict (pi1_data M)=). These
  are NOT shims — they're field projections from the Record, so all
  existing client code (=monodromy=, =riemann_hilbert_surjective=,
  =gl1_geometric_langlands=) continues to compile unchanged. No
  axiom-tax.
- Net delta: -2 shallow-Type-tag Parameters, +1 Record-typed
  Parameter, +1 Record =Pi1Group= definition.

WHY THE OTHER FILES STAYED UNTOUCHED:
- =BeilinsonBernstein.v=: =FlagVariety=, =DLambdaModule=, =UgModuleCC=,
  =LineBundle_lambda=, =TwistedDOp=, =global_sections= are exactly
  the "deep structural objects best left as opaque carriers" from
  the task's exclusion list — they're moduli/sheaves/D-modules
  associated with paper-attributable theorems (Beilinson-Bernstein,
  Borel-Weil-Bott, Harish-Chandra). Bundling them would either
  fabricate axioms or destroy abstraction.
- =NonabelianHodge.v=: =HasVanishingChernClasses=, =HasHarmonicMetric=,
  =HasHiggsHarmonicMetric= are =Prop=-valued predicates on existing
  Record types (=HiggsBundle=, =LocalSystem=). They're not Type
  tags. =flat_to_higgs= and =higgs_to_flat= are operations whose
  codomain is already a Record (=HiggsBundle= / =LocalSystem=).
  Each predicate is surrounded by Conjectures that constrain its
  behaviour (=flat_to_higgs_stable=, =flat_to_higgs_vanishing=,
  =flat_to_higgs_rank=, =higgs_to_flat_rank=). Directive-compliant
  as-is.
- =AbelianLanglands.v=: only Parameter =ls_trivial : forall M,
  LocalSystem M= — codomain is the =LocalSystem= Record. Already
  bundled.

** DONE Task C.0 — Add omega_pow_apart axiom + close geometric_sum_nonzero [γ R4 — 2026-05-01]
SCOPE: =theories/NeuralOp/DFT.v= only
ESTIMATE: 30-45 min (delivered; some prior groundwork already on disk from earlier round)
- [X] Added sound axiom =omega_pow_apart= at DFT.v:268-272.
      Final form (chosen to match what =Cinv= consumes; equivalent to the
      spec form =Csub C1 (Cpow (omega N) k) #C C0= since =#C= unfolds to
      =Cnorm2 (Csub _ _) # 0=, but without the redundant outer =Csub _ C0=):
      #+BEGIN_SRC coq
      Axiom omega_pow_apart : forall (N k : nat),
          N <> 0%nat -> k mod N <> 0%nat ->
          Cnorm2 (Csub C1 (Cpow (omega N) k)) # 0.
      #+END_SRC
      One-line justification: "standard classical-analysis fact that
      distinct primitive roots of unity are apart in [CReal] (squared
      norm 2(1 − cos(2π k/N)) is strictly positive when k mod N ≠ 0)".
- [X] Telescoping helper [gsum_at_telescope_req] proven:
      (C1 - ω^k) * gsum_at Nfix n k ~~C ω^0 - ω^(n*k) by induction on n.
- [X] [omega_pow_Nk] proven (Cpow (omega N) (N*k) = Cpow C1 k via Cpow_mul + omega_pow).
- [X] [geometric_sum_nonzero] converted from Axiom to Lemma at DFT.v:395-444.
      Proof outline:
        1. Rewrite the [fix sumω] sum to [gsum_at N N k] via [sumω_eq_gsum_at_req].
        2. Set D = C1 - ω^k; obtain HD : Cnorm2 D # 0 from omega_pow_apart.
        3. Apply telescoping: D * gsum_at N N k ~~C ω^0 - ω^(N*k) = C1 - C1 = C0.
        4. Multiply by Cinv D HD: gsum_at = Cinv D HD * (D * gsum_at) = Cinv D HD * C0 = C0.
- [X] [geometric_sum_zero] (sibling case k mod N = 0) was already a Lemma
      from a prior round (uses [omega_pow_multiple] + [sumω_const_C1]).
- [X] =rocq compile -Q theories CAG theories/NeuralOp/DFT.v= exits 0.
- [X] =Print Assumptions geometric_sum_nonzero= depends on:
      =omega_pow_apart=, =exp_i_2pi=, =exp_i_zero=, =exp_i_add=, =exp_i_neg=,
      =exp_i= (Param), =pi_R= (Param), =CRealEq_eq= bridge.
      No transitive dependencies on residual axioms beyond these.
DELIVERED: =geometric_sum_nonzero= Axiom → Lemma; net axiom delta in DFT.v
is 0 (=geometric_sum_nonzero= replaced by =omega_pow_apart=), but the new
axiom is provably sound (paper-attributable to standard CReal apartness
of cos(2π k/N) from 1) and is shared with potential future apartness
witnesses, while the old =geometric_sum_nonzero= axiom was a derived
identity that hard-coded an entire telescoping argument. Net soundness
strictly improved.

** Reclassification: A.3 + A.4 → Tier 3 long-haul

After α-A.3 diagnosis, the gluing axioms (`gluing_data_exists`, `I_is_full`, `I_is_faithful`)
and Conservativity.v axioms are not subtask-level. They require either:
- (a) Build presheaf functor T + discharge Gluing.v Parameters (multi-day)
- (b) Build βη-normalisation procedure on AxTerm (multi-day, alternative)

Either is a multi-day effort comparable to DG/LM/SP. Moved to Tier 3.

DIAGNOSIS / RECOMMENDED NEXT STEP:
The var case demonstrates the proof pattern works.  The app case
should follow the SAME pattern:
1. Unfold [interp_term_data_app_explicit] on LHS to get
   [md_fun (GenericModelTh_data Th) f ∘ fp_tuple ...].

   [GenericModelTh_mod_fun] (a transport of [clth_mk_q (G_fun Sg f)]).

   past the quotient projection; the underlying clmor_terms is
   [[t_app f args]].

   [ClMor_theq]-equivalent (via the substitution-cong rule
   [theq_subst_cong] applied per argument; argument-IH provides
   [clmor_terms = [args[i]]]).

(~30 LoC combined).

** Top-5 tractable candidates (ranked, NOT in hammer_attempted, not
   in α/β territory)

Caveat: every candidate below has a structural obstruction that
explains why it's still open — but each is plausibly a 30-min to
1-hr closure under the right strategy.  None is a trivial 5-minute
collapse.

1. =Cinv_mul_right=, =Cinv_mul_left= (theories/ComplexAnalysis.v:284-285)
   - Statement: =Cmul z (Cinv z) = C1=, =Cmul (Cinv z) z = C1=
     (under hypothesis =Cnorm2 z # 0=).
   - Difficulty: M.  =Cinv= is still a =Parameter= here (line 282).
     Cycle 32 (memory) describes a successful Cinv construction
     pattern (=Cinv_compute= + =Cinv_eq_compute= bridge) that does NOT
     appear in either =Complex.v= or =ComplexAnalysis.v= as of R13.
     Re-applying that pattern to =ComplexAnalysis.v= (=Cinv_compute=
     concrete Definition + bridge axiom) would close both Conjectures
     in ~30-45 min.
   - Reward: closes 2 Conjectures + unlocks =Cdiv= simplifications.
   - Risk: requires adding 1 new bridge axiom; net would still be
     −1 if it closes 2 Conjectures (Conjecture is an open-assumption
     equivalent in our accounting, so net assumption count stays flat).

2. =circle_path_dist=, =circle_path_at_0= (theories/ComplexAnalysis.v)
   - Statement: =Cdist2 (circle_path z0 r t) z0 = r * r=,
     =circle_path z0 r 0 = z0 + r=.
   - Difficulty: S/M.  =circle_path= is Definition; both should compute.
     Likely =unfold; CComplex_eq; ring= via Cycle-27 ring infrastructure.
   - Rationale: cycle 27/28 already added =Add Ring CComplex_ring= and
     numerous =C0=/=C1= mul/add laws.  These two should fall to it.

3. =trivial_FIS=-style: =hall_M_strong_free_factor= post-vacuity check
   (=theories/DecisionProblems/HallTheorem.v=)
   - Difficulty: S.  Cycle 11–13 strengthened it; verify it's now
     vacuously satisfiable like the parent and convert.
   - Rationale: same pattern that closed =hall_finite_index_free_factor=.
   - Status: needs re-reading the strengthened =r ≥ 2 ∧ fis_index ≥ 2=
     hypothesis to confirm trivial_FIS still satisfies it.

4. =Pic_iso_Z_trivial= (theories/Projective/HyperplaneBundle.v)
   - Statement: =Pic_iso_Z n (hlb_trivial (CPn_cm n)) = 0%Z=.
   - Difficulty: M.  =Pic_iso_Z= and =hlb_trivial= are both Parameters,
     so cannot be discharged without making one concrete.
   - Status: defer — requires Parameter→Definition refactor (similar
     to cycle 28's =Vm_mod=).

5. =free_gen_RWord_not_conj_inv=-derivative work:
   =distinct_generators_not_conjugate= variants in
   =theories/DecisionProblems/WordLengthFreeGroup.v=
   - Already cycle-42b discharged 5 in this family; check if more
     can be added under the cycle-24 =expsum_word_i= machinery.
   - Difficulty: S–M.  Pattern is established.

6. =sobolev_norm_zero_is_L2= / =sobolev_norm_nonneg= /
   =sobolev_norm_monotone= (theories/Harmonic/Sobolev.v)
   - Difficulty: M.  =sobolev_norm= is Parameter; needs concrete
     definition (e.g. =:= 0%CReal=) to discharge in trivial-zero model.
   - Risk: changing =sobolev_norm= to a concrete Definition is a
     refactor with cross-file implications.  Verify zero-model works
     end-to-end before committing.
   - Reward: would close 3 conjectures in one go.

7. =L2_inner_zero_iff= (theories/Harmonic/Sobolev.v)
   - Difficulty: L (false in trivial-zero model — would need
     non-trivial L2 model).  SKIP.

8. =CReal_nonneg_sum_zero_both= (theories/Harmonic/Sobolev.v)
   - Statement: =0 <= a → 0 <= b → a + b = 0 → a = 0 ∧ b = 0=.
   - Difficulty: L.  Comment in file says "not provable without
     additional axioms (Qeq form would be derivable)".  SKIP.

9. =matrix-axioms in Lie/Symplectic.v= (=mat_transpose_mul=, etc.)
   - OFF-LIMITS — Lie territory, Task M.0/M.1/M.2 reserved for α/β.

10. =order_pq_classification= (theories/Groups/SemidirectProduct.v)
    - Famous old (groups of order pq).  SKIP per axiom-priority memory.

** Why no Step-3 closure this round

Tried — every candidate that passed the territory + 30-min file-edit
filter turned out to be either (i) a Parameter-spec Conjecture that
needs the Parameter to be made concrete first (Sobolev, Garding,
HyperplaneBundle), (ii) a trivial-zero-model Conjecture whose
statement is *false* in that model and so can't be discharged trivially
(=L2_inner_pos=, =L2_inner_zero_iff=), or (iii) famous-old / paper-
attributable that the priority memory rules out.

The hammer_attempted.txt list (744 entries) contains essentially all
of the structurally-trivial axioms; the 27 not-hammered names are
mostly Parameters (=Chain=, =Current=, =DeRhamCohom=, =HomologyQ=,
=HomologyZ=, =betti=, =hq_add=, etc.) that don't even have conjecture
form.

Recommendation for next round (R14):

A. Concrete refactor on =sobolev_norm := 0%CReal=.  Closes 3
   conjectures (=sobolev_norm_zero_is_L2=, =_nonneg=, =_monotone=)
   plus possibly =garding_c=/=garding_C0= if they admit a similar
   trivial-positive-constant model.  Estimated ~30-60 min, single
   file =theories/Harmonic/Sobolev.v= + verify-only chain into
   Garding.v.  Stays out of α/β territory.

B. Verify =Cinv_mul_right=/=Cinv_mul_left= are stale Conjectures
   left over from before cycle 32's =Cinv_eq_compute= bridge.  If
   so, convert to Lemmas using the cycle-32 pattern.  ~15 min.

C. Re-audit =hall_M_strong_free_factor= for vacuity.  ~10 min.

These three steps could plausibly close 5 conjectures + 2 axioms in
a single round if all go through.

** DONE =Cinv_mul_right=, =Cinv_mul_left= (Conjecture → Lemma)

Resurrected cycle 32's pattern in =theories/ComplexAnalysis.v= (the
prior cycle-32 work was apparently lost in the cycle-41 cleanup — no
trace remained as of R13 audit).

Edits in =theories/ComplexAnalysis.v= (around line 282 onward):
- Added =Definition Cinv_compute (z : CComplex) (h : Cnorm2 z # 0) :
  CComplex := mkC (re z * (/ Cnorm2 z) h) ((- im z) * (/ Cnorm2 z) h)=
  — identical formula to =CAG.Complex.Cinv= but locally re-stated
  (the parameter shadow makes the qualified form awkward).
- Added single bridge =Axiom Cinv_eq_compute : forall z h, Cinv z =
  Cinv_compute z h=.  This is the ONLY new global axiom and is sound
  in the standard model (both sides equal =(re z - i·im z)/Cnorm2 z=).
- Added two helper Lemmas =Cinv_compute_mul_right= /
  =Cinv_compute_mul_left= via componentwise =CRealEq= + =CReal_inv_r=
  + =CComplex_eq= bridge from =Complex.v= (cycle 17).
- Converted =Cinv_mul_right= and =Cinv_mul_left= from =Conjecture= to
  =Lemma=; one-liner proofs via =rewrite (Cinv_eq_compute z h)=.

Compile evidence: =rocq compile -Q theories CAG theories/ComplexAnalysis.v=
exit 0.  =theories/ComplexAnalysis2.v= still compiles clean (verified
independently).

=Print Assumptions Cinv_mul_right= / =Cinv_mul_left= each show:
- =Cinv : CComplex -> CComplex= (the file's own Parameter — expected),
- =Cinv_eq_compute= (the new bridge — expected),
- =Complex.CRealEq_eq= (project-wide setoid bridge — expected,
  long-standing axiom).
No extraneous dependencies.

Net delta: −2 Conjectures, +1 Axiom, +2 Lemmas, +1 Definition.
Open-assumption count: −1 (Conjectures and Axioms both count).

** BLOCKED =circle_path_dist=, =circle_path_at_0=

R13 audit assumed =circle_path= was a =Definition=; it is in fact a
=Parameter= (=theories/ComplexAnalysis.v:293=).  The two Conjectures
function as the *spec axioms* for that Parameter.  Without sin/cos in
scope (the file's stated reason for parameterizing), no concrete
realiser is available that simultaneously:
  (i)  satisfies =Cdist2 (circle_path z0 r t) z0 = r * r= for all =t=
       (every point on the circle of radius =r= around =z0=),
  (ii) makes the downstream =cauchy_integral_formula= Conjecture
       *true* (a closed contour traversal of the boundary).

Specifically:
- A constant choice =circle_path z0 r t := Cadd z0 (mkC r 0)= would
  satisfy both Conjectures trivially BUT make =cauchy_integral_formula=
  provably false (constant path → integral = 0 ≠ 2πi·f(z) generically).
- The Weierstrass rational parameterization satisfies the spec but is
  a non-closed arc on =[0,1]=, also breaking
  =cauchy_integral_formula=.
- A spec-bundling refactor (1 stronger Parameter carrying the
  conjunction) reduces Conjecture count by 2 and adds 1 Parameter,
  net −1 open assumption — but the discharge is structural rather
  than mathematical.  Deferred for now since it doesn't increase
  honest content.

Documented and left as Conjectures.  Genuine discharge requires
defining sin/cos (constructive series, deep) or accepting that the
spec axioms are paper-attributable boundary parameterization
primitives.

** Cumulative

This round: −2 Conjectures, +1 Axiom (the =Cinv_eq_compute= bridge),
+1 Definition, +4 Lemmas (two helpers + the two ex-Conjectures).
Net open-assumption delta: −1.  Single-file compile verified.

* DONE Axiomatization rework — Lebesgue measure [β R13 — 2026-05-01]

Continuation of the user's axiomatization directive on
[theories/Measure/Lebesgue.v], following the γ R24 Sobolev / γ R25
[L2_inner] / γ R26 [hilbert_inner] template.

** Decision: Option A (revert) for the measure object; preserve §3-§4
   box-volume infrastructure (Option B in spirit).

Audit findings before revert:
- The =Definition Lebesgue : forall n, Measure (trivial_sigma (Cn n))=
  was a concrete witness on the {∅, full_set} σ-algebra: empty ↦ 0,
  full ↦ +∞.  The three "basic property" Theorems
  ([Lebesgue_empty_zero], [Lebesgue_full_inf], [Lebesgue_nonneg])
  were trivial-collapse on this 2-element σ-algebra and conveyed no
  Lebesgue-specific content.
- =grep -rn= over =theories/= shows NO file consumes =Lebesgue= /
  =trivial_sigma= / =lebesgue_meas_fn= / any of the §1-§2 / §3 (post)
  trivial-σ-algebra lemmas externally — they are pure scaffolding
  for the trivial-collapse measure object.
- The ONLY exported items consumed downstream are the box-volume
  infrastructure: =CBox=, =mkCBox=, =cbox_re_lo / cbox_re_hi /
  cbox_im_lo / cbox_im_hi=, and =unit_cbox= (used by =AG.v= and
  =Calc/Integration.v=).  These have honest CReal arithmetic
  content (NOT trivial-collapse): Option B applies to them.

** DONE Replace the trivial-σ Lebesgue measure with abstract
   Parameter + defining Axioms.

[theories/Measure/Lebesgue.v]:
- Removed =Definition Lebesgue (n : nat) : Measure (trivial_sigma (Cn n))=.
- Added 4 new =Parameter=s (each with informal-definition comment):
  =lebesgue_sigma_alg= (Lebesgue σ-algebra on Cn n), =LebesgueMeasure=
  (the abstract Lebesgue measure), =box_subset= (CBox → Subset Cn n
  inclusion), =set_translate= (set translation by a vector).
- Added 5 new defining =Axiom=s (each with informal-definition comment):
  | Axiom name                          | Informal statement                                    |
  |-------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------------|
  | =box_in_sigma=                      | A box is Lebesgue-measurable                          |
  | =translate_in_sigma=                | Translates of measurable sets are measurable          |
  | =Lebesgue_box_volume=               | μ(box B) = lebesgue_box_volume B (Folland Thm 1.16)   |
  | =Lebesgue_translation_invariant=    | μ(A + v) = μ(A) (Folland Thm 2.42 / Bogachev 1.4.4)   |
  | =Lebesgue_full_is_inf=              | μ(R^{2n}) = +∞                                        |

** DONE Convert trivial-collapse Theorems to Axioms.

| Name                  | Status before β R13 | Status after β R13                              |
|-----------------------+---------------------+-------------------------------------------------|
| =Lebesgue_empty_zero= | Theorem (trivial)   | Axiom (over abstract LebesgueMeasure)           |
| =Lebesgue_full_inf=   | Theorem (trivial)   | Renamed to =Lebesgue_full_is_inf= Axiom         |
| =Lebesgue_nonneg=     | Theorem (trivial)   | Axiom                                           |

Each new Axiom carries an immediately-preceding informal-definition
comment block.  Empty-set null is automatic from the [Measure]
record's =meas_empty= field (so the Axiom is provable as a Lemma but
restated for documentation parity); non-negativity is automatic
from the type [NNExtCReal]; both were trivial-collapse Theorems on
the {∅, full_set} σ-algebra prior to revert.

** DONE Rename =Lebesgue_translation_invariant= (box version) →
   =Lebesgue_translation_invariant_box=.

The §3 (formerly §4) =Theorem Lebesgue_translation_invariant= had
the box-arithmetic statement
  =lebesgue_box_volume (cbox_translate B t) == lebesgue_box_volume B=
(Leibniz-prop CReal equality).  Renamed to add the [_box] suffix to
disambiguate from the new abstract-measure-level
=Lebesgue_translation_invariant= Axiom.  The renamed theorem retains
its full constructive proof (uses =vol_aux_translate= +
=cancel_translate=) and remains axiom-free over Stdlib.

** DONE Preserve all honest box-volume + σ-algebra-closure content.

Per [feedback_dead_math.md] ("never strip non-equivalent theorems"),
the following honest constructive lemmas are RETAINED in the file
even though they are no longer load-bearing for the abstract
=LebesgueMeasure=:
- §1: =trivial_meas=, =trivial_empty=, =trivial_compl=, =trivial_cu=,
  =trivial_sigma= — σ-algebra closure on {∅, full_set}.
- §2: =lebesgue_meas_fn=, =lebesgue_meas_empty=, =cu_all_empty=,
  =cu_some_full=, =lebesgue_pointwise_all_empty=, =chain_zero_creal=,
  =chain_zero_creal_eq_zero=, =nne_partial_sum_all_zero_chain=,
  =nne_series_all_zero_to_zero=, =nne_partial_sum_after_inf=,
  =classical_some_full=, =lebesgue_countable_add= — constructive
  σ-additivity on the 2-element σ-algebra.
- §3: =CBox= record, =mkCBox= constructor + accessors, =enum_fin=,
  =vol_aux=, =lebesgue_box_volume=, =unit_cbox=,
  =vol_aux_unit_constant_1=, =Lebesgue_unit_box= (unit-box volume = 1
  — real CReal arithmetic), =cbox_translate=, =cancel_translate=,
  =vol_aux_translate=, =Lebesgue_translation_invariant_box=.
- §4: =Lebesgue_dim0_volume=, =vol_aux_step=, =enum_fin_length=.

These have honest CReal/list/Fin arithmetic content; the box-volume
ones are exported (used by =AG.v= and =Calc/Integration.v=); the
σ-algebra-closure ones are kept for completeness.

* DONE Lebesgue Axioms tightened via Measure Record field projections [β R15 — 2026-05-01]

Follow-up to β R13 implementing the user's stronger directive in
[feedback_bundled_records.md]: "when a [Measure] Record exists,
its laws should be field projections, not floating Axioms."

** Audit of the 7 β R13 Axioms in [theories/Measure/Lebesgue.v]

| Name                              | Status after β R15 | Reason                                                  |
|-----------------------------------+--------------------+---------------------------------------------------------|
| =Lebesgue_box_volume=             | Kept Axiom         | Lebesgue-specific (Folland Thm 1.16); not a generic Measure law |
| =Lebesgue_translation_invariant=  | Kept Axiom         | Lebesgue-specific (Folland Thm 2.42); not a generic Measure law |
| =Lebesgue_full_is_inf=            | Kept Axiom         | Lebesgue-specific value (μ(R^{2n}) = +∞)                |
| =box_in_sigma=                    | Kept Axiom         | Membership fact about the [box_subset] Parameter        |
| =translate_in_sigma=              | Kept Axiom         | Membership fact about the [set_translate] Parameter     |
| =Lebesgue_empty_zero=             | Converted to Lemma | Discharged by =meas_empty (LebesgueMeasure n)= field proj |
| =Lebesgue_nonneg=                 | Kept Axiom (β R15); converted to Lemma in β R17 | β R15: =Measure= Record had no =meas_nonneg= field.  β R17 added the field and converted to a 1-line projection Lemma. |

The =Measure= Record fields in [theories/Measure/Basic.v:253-265]
are: =meas_fn=, =meas_empty=, =meas_countable_add=.  The codomain
=NNExtCReal= does not enforce non-negativity intrinsically (the
=NNFin= constructor admits any =CReal=), so non-negativity is NOT
derivable without either a new Record field or a separate Lemma.
Per [feedback_bundled_records.md]'s constraint ("If the [Measure]
Record doesn't have the relevant law as a field, leave the Axiom
in place"), Record-extension is out of scope for β R15 and
=Lebesgue_nonneg= remains an Axiom.

** New Lemma added

[theories/Measure/Lebesgue.v:707-714] — =Lebesgue_empty_zero=
(formerly Axiom; now Lemma).  One-line proof:

#+BEGIN_SRC coq
Lemma Lebesgue_empty_zero :
  forall n,
    meas_fn (LebesgueMeasure n) empty_set
            (sigma_empty (lebesgue_sigma_alg n))
    = nne_zero.
Proof. intro n. exact (meas_empty (LebesgueMeasure n)). Qed.
#+END_SRC

The proof is a pure field projection: the bundled =LebesgueMeasure n=
already carries the =meas_empty= proof obligation at construction
time, so projecting that field out gives the desired equation.

** Compile evidence

=rocq compile -Q theories CAG theories/Measure/Lebesgue.v= → exit 0.

** =Print Assumptions= confirmation

Probe file imports =Measure.Lebesgue= and prints assumptions for
each of the 7 β R13 Axioms / Lemmas:

- =Lebesgue_empty_zero= → references only =LebesgueMeasure= and
  =lebesgue_sigma_alg= (the bundled Parameters).  NO floating
  Axiom dependence — this is the structural improvement.
- =Lebesgue_box_volume=, =Lebesgue_translation_invariant=,
  =Lebesgue_full_is_inf=, =Lebesgue_nonneg=, =box_in_sigma=,
  =translate_in_sigma= → each reports itself as a top-level
  Axiom (correct: each is genuinely Lebesgue-specific or
  parametric and not derivable from generic [Measure] Record
  laws).

* DONE =Measure= Record carries =meas_nonneg= field [β R17 — 2026-05-01]

Follow-up to β R15.  Closes the gap noted in β R15: the previous
[=Measure=] Record had three fields ([=meas_fn=], [=meas_empty=],
[=meas_countable_add=]) but no non-negativity law, which forced

** Cascade audit

A grep for [=Build_Measure=] / [=mkMeasure=] / [=: Measure =] over
[theories/] revealed exactly **one** [=Measure=] instance in the
whole codebase: the abstract [=Parameter LebesgueMeasure=] at
[theories/Measure/Lebesgue.v:633].  [=Measure/Probability.v=]'s
[=ps_meas : Measure ps_sigma=] is a Record field declaration, not
a constructor invocation, and no concrete [=mkProbSpace=] is built
anywhere downstream.  Cascade scope is therefore minimal — well
under the BAIL threshold of 5 instances.

** Record extension

[theories/Measure/Basic.v:253-275] — added a fourth field

#+begin_src coq
  meas_nonneg :
    forall (A : Subset X) (HA : sigma_in S A),
      nne_le nne_zero (meas_fn A HA);
#+end_src

with [Arguments meas_nonneg {X S} _ _ _.] alongside the existing
field-arg declarations.  Rationale: the codomain [=NNExtCReal=] is
a syntactic envelope only — its [=NNFin=] constructor admits any
[=CReal=], including negative values — so the non-negativity
constraint must live at the Record level if it is to be
projection-derivable.

** Instance updates

Only [=LebesgueMeasure=] needed updating, and as a Parameter no
explicit construction is required: the new field is automatically
part of the Parameter's type signature.

** =Lebesgue_nonneg= conversion

[theories/Measure/Lebesgue.v:723-728] — was

#+begin_src coq
Axiom Lebesgue_nonneg :
  forall n (A : Subset (Cn n)) (HA : sigma_in (lebesgue_sigma_alg n) A),
    nne_le nne_zero (meas_fn (LebesgueMeasure n) A HA).
#+end_src

now

#+begin_src coq
Lemma Lebesgue_nonneg :
  forall n (A : Subset (Cn n)) (HA : sigma_in (lebesgue_sigma_alg n) A),
    nne_le nne_zero (meas_fn (LebesgueMeasure n) A HA).
Proof. intros n A HA. exact (meas_nonneg (LebesgueMeasure n) A HA). Qed.
#+end_src

** DONE Convert trivial-collapse Lemmas back to Axioms (Sobolev.v)

* DONE Axiomatization rework — Sobolev test case [γ R24 — 2026-05-01]

User design directive (received pre-R24): the trivial-zero design
pattern is busywork, not rigor — see feedbacks
[feedback_trivial_collapse_busywork.md] +
[feedback_axiomatize_parameters.md].  Bare Parameters are opaque
tags; trivial-zero "discharges" satisfy the typechecker but vacate
the abstraction.  New pattern: keep [Parameter X : T], surround it
with [Axiom]s that constrain its behavior, comment each Axiom with
its informal mathematical English statement.  R24 is the test case;
if successful, the pattern will be replicated on [L2_inner],
[Lebesgue], [hilbert_inner], etc.

* AUDIT γ R16 — DecisionProblems sweep, no closures [2026-05-01]

Read-only audit of =theories/DecisionProblems/= (rotation Round 16,
concurrent with α on ATT/L.3 app-case and β on Lie/Linear matrix
axioms).  Outcome: no closures; all candidate axioms/conjectures are
either paper-attributable, structurally blocked, or already proved.

** =hall_M_strong_free_factor= vacuity re-audit (Step 1)

Verdict: NOT vacuous in the cycle-11 sense, NOT discharged.

- Statement (=HallTheorem.v:2515=): for =r ≥ 2= and =gamma ≠ e=,
  exists =FIS : FiniteIndexSubgroup (FreeGroup r)= with =fis_index ≥ 2=
  containing both =gamma= and =e=.
- Precondition =r ≥ 2 ∧ gamma ≠ e= IS achievable: take =r := 2=,
  =gamma := free_gen_RWord 2 F1=.  So unlike cycle-11's
  =hall_finite_index_free_factor= shape, the implication body must
  actually be inhabited.
- Conclusion requires a witness FIS with =fis_index ≥ 2=.  The only
  FIS constructor in the project is =trivial_FIS= (=fis_index = 1=).
  Building an index-2 FIS (kernel of abelianization mod 2 is the
  natural choice) requires: predicate =fun w => Z.even (expsum_i F1 w)=,
  size-2 transversal, fis_trans_dec (every word is in one of two
  cosets), fis_pred_dec (Z.even is decidable), fis_trans_unique
  (the two cosets are distinct).  All doable mechanically, but
  it's a substantive ~200-line construction — explicitly out of
  scope per task constraint "If requires deep group theory, leave
  as Axiom".
- Additional reason to leave intact: =hall_M_strong_free_factor= is
  declared =Conjecture= (not =Axiom=) and the task constraint
  "Don't touch =Conjecture= declarations" applies.  Cycle-11
  precedent for =hall_finite_index_free_factor= was that the precond
  reduced to =True ∨ False= over a degenerate =r ∈ {0, 1}= split;
  the strong form excludes those cases by construction so the same
  trick doesn't apply.

** Step 2 — Axiom hunt in DecisionProblems/

Found exactly 2 standing =Axiom= declarations in =DecisionProblems/=:

1. =Z_coset_equivalent_same_order_multiset= (=FiniteLifts.v:950=).
   Burnside / table-of-marks argument; paper-attributable to standard
   group-theory references (Dummit & Foote Ch. 4-5 territory).
   Statement quantifies over =element_order_multiset=, itself a
   =Parameter= — so this Axiom is partly a spec-axiom for that
   Parameter.  Discharging would require giving =element_order_multiset=
   a concrete Definition, which (as the file comment notes) requires
   =order_of= and finite enumeration of the subgroup — substantive
   refactor.  Leave intact.

2. =free_conjugacy_decision_thm= (=WordLengthFreeGroup.v:676=).
   Magnus-Karass-Solitar cyclic-reduction algorithm.  Famous old
   result; per axiom-priority memory ("skip famous old theorems"),
   leave intact.

Conjectures inventory (=21= total): all paper-attributable open
research problems — KLMRS theorems 1.6/1.7, Bass-Lubotzky
specialization, Lawton-Louder-McReynolds 1.13, Hall theorem variants,
McReynolds-Lawton-Louder Theorem 1.6 / 3.1 / 3.2 / corollary 1.2
(uniform decidability variants for free / surface groups).  All
explicitly excluded by task constraints.

Parameters inventory (=19= total): all are spec-only carriers for
external concepts (=NumberField=, =MCG=, =MaxNonArithLattice=,
=profinite_completion=, =element_order_multiset=, =R_coset_equivalent=,
=is_continuous_hom=, =IsProfinite=, =IsSurfaceGroup=, etc.).  Each
would require deep mathematical infrastructure to make concrete.

  The cycle-42b sweep was complete as of cycle 42b.

* Top-level theories/ Axiom re-audit [γ R18 — 2026-05-01]

** Axiom inventory (depth-1 =theories/*.v=, excluding territories)

After AG.v (β territory) and LieAlgebra.v (β territory) and ATT/AxTheory
(α territory) are removed, exactly 4 Axioms remain in scope:

1. =theories/Complex.v:610= — =CRealEq_eq : forall x y : CReal, CRealEq x y -> x = y=
2. =theories/ComplexAnalysis.v:121= — =Cderiv_witness : (CComplex -> CComplex) -> CComplex -> CComplex=
3. =theories/ComplexAnalysis.v:123= — =Cderiv_witness_correct : forall f z L, Cderiv_at f z L -> Cequal (Cderiv_witness f z) L=
4. =theories/ComplexAnalysis.v:299= — =Cinv_eq_compute : forall z h, Cinv z = Cinv_compute z h=

(The 8th candidate from R13 was =Complex.v:610= + =ComplexAnalysis.v= ×3
plus AG.v ×3 + the original =NeuralOp/DFT= shadow; the AG.v ones are
β territory now and the rest had already migrated. 4 in scope.)

** Status assessment

All 4 candidates are paper-attributable / structurally axiomatic; none
admits a trivial-discharge or vacuous closure.

| Axiom                  | hammer-attempted | classification             |
|------------------------+------------------+----------------------------|
| =CRealEq_eq=           | yes              | paper-attributable         |
| =Cderiv_witness=       | yes              | paper-attributable         |
| =Cderiv_witness_correct= | yes            | paper-attributable         |
| =Cinv_eq_compute=      | no               | paper-attributable         |

Detailed reasoning:

- =CRealEq_eq= is the cycle-17 Tier 1.A foundational bridge: setoid-
  equality on Cauchy reals ⇒ Leibniz equality.  Proves equivalent to
  functional+propositional extensionality on the constructive Cauchy
  rep.  Removing it un-discharges ~17 lemmas across LieAlgebra.v / AG.v
  (project_state cycle 17 + 21).  Hammer attempted (sha 145e216eb1ab).
  KEEP — paper-attributable extensionality.

- =Cderiv_witness= / =Cderiv_witness_correct= are Hilbert ε / definite-
  description on CReal limits.  Same structural pattern as
  =partial_zbar_witness= / =partial_z_witness= in =Calc/Forms.v=.  Both
  hammer-attempted (sha b86506bfc962, 3896dd668b61).  KEEP —
  paper-attributable classical analysis primitive.

- =Cinv_eq_compute= is the bridge between the =Parameter Cinv= shadow
  (no apartness arg) and the concrete =Cinv_compute= (with apartness
  arg).  The shadow exists because =Cinv= is used inside =Cdiv= and
  the Cauchy formula contexts where the apartness witness isn't
  threaded through.  Discharge would require either replacing
  =Parameter Cinv= with a constructive total =Definition= (impossible:
  =Cnorm2 z # 0= is not decidable in Set), or accepting classical EM
  (a worse global axiom).  Not hammer-attempted because the proof
  obstruction is type-level, not search-space.  KEEP — paper-
  attributable model-soundness bridge.

** Why no Step-3 closure this round

Every in-scope axiom is structurally axiomatic.  The R13 audit
already noted that "62 remaining Axioms are now almost all paper-
attributable or intentionally-deep"; R14-R17 closed the remaining
tractable ones.  The 4 here are all in the =almost all= class.
Audit-only round.  No source files modified.  No compile invocations
needed (no .v changes).

** Net delta this round
0.  Audit only; no closures, no new axioms, no new lemmas.

* AUDIT γ R19 — Vanishing/Hodge/Kodaira/Blowup/Divisor sweep, no closures [2026-05-01]

following γ R8 / R12 / R15 pattern.

** Conjecture inventory (5 directories, 30 total)

| File                                         | Conj. | Statement-shape       |
|----------------------------------------------+-------+-----------------------|
| =Vanishing/KodairaVanishing.v=               |     4 | =HDolb=-equality      |
| =Vanishing/RestrictionToHyperplane.v=        |     4 | =HDolb=-equality      |

| =Vanishing/TheoremB.v=                       |     2 | =HDolb=-equality      |

| =Kodaira/Embedding.v=                        |     1 | =kodaira_map= inj.    |
| =Kodaira/SeparationOfTangents.v=             |     1 | =HDolb=-equality      |
| =Kodaira/RationalKahlerCriterion.v=          |     1 | =positive_line_b=     |

| =Blowup/CurvatureExceptional.v=              |     1 | =positive_line_b=     |
| =Blowup/ExceptionalDivisor.v=                |     2 | =km_dim=-of-blowup    |
| =Divisor/Curvature.v=                        |     1 | =Cequal= ∂̄(curv) C0   |
| =Divisor/LineBundleCech.v=                   |     3 | =hlb_iso= w/ bare =L= |
| =Divisor/RiemannSurfaceDegree.v=             |     3 | =Z=-equality          |

Total: 30 Conjectures.

** Classification: 0 collapses

Every Conjecture in the 5 surveyed directories falls into one of three
non-collapse categories:

1. *Opaque-=Parameter= obstruction* (~24 of 30): the statement equates
   elements of a =Parameter=-typed family that has no zero-collapse
   Definition.  =HDolb=, =HdR=, =HermitianMetric=, =divisor_class=,
   =kodaira_map=, =H2Z_pair_surface=, =partial_zbar_witness=,
   =pullback_lb=, =canonical_bundle=, =exceptional_line_bundle=,
   =blowup=, =restriction_dolbeault=, =les_star_map= are all
   =Parameter=s.  The trivial-zero pattern doesn't reach them, so
   their cohomology / divisor / curvature equalities cannot be reduced
   to syntactic equalities.  Example: =serre_duality_vanishing=
   states a =<->= between =HDolb=-zeroness on two parameter types;
   neither side reduces.

2. *Bare =L= on RHS / arbitrary-input shape* (3 of 30):
   =hlb_tensor_trivial=, =hlb_dual_dual= (=LineBundleCech.v=
   209/220), =smooth_line_bundles_classified_by_c1= (=:279=).  LHS
   reduces to =hlb_trivial M= via the empty-cover collapse, but RHS
   contains the free =L=.  =hlb_iso= is generated by =refl/symm/trans=
   constructors only — no constructor produces =hlb_iso (hlb_trivial
   M) L= for arbitrary L.  =LineBundleCech.v= itself documents this
   explicitly at lines 187-198: "=hlb_tensor_trivial= and =hlb_dual_dual=
   mention bare =L=, so they require the abstract relation; we leave
   those as Conjectures."

3. *Existential of Parameter inhabitant* (3 of 30):
   =rational_class_to_integral= (=RationalKahlerCriterion.v:55=),
   =positivity_of_pullback_minus_exceptional_divisor= (=CurvatureExceptional.v:97=),
   =positive_twist_plus_canonical= (=CanonicalBundle.v:70=).  Each
   concludes =positive_line_bundle ... L'= which unfolds to
   =exists h : HermitianMetric ... L', True=.  The hypothesis gives a
   metric on a *different* bundle / manifold; no transport lemma
   exists and =HermitianMetric= is opaque, so the existential cannot
   be discharged.

** Specifically NOT-FALSE-under-trivial-zero (per γ R8 / R12 caveat)

Spot-checked the 30 statements for the "trivially false" caveat:
none of them flip to FALSE under the trivial-zero Definitions
(unlike =rough_laplacian_pos=-style statements in =Harmonic/=).
They all either remain provable-in-genuine-theory and unprovable-
here, or are stated as vanishing/equality which is neutral under
collapse.  No "trivial-zero kills it" Conjectures in this scope —
nothing to flag for caution, nothing to discharge.

** Why nothing collapses here

The 5 directories were specifically refactored in earlier rounds
(=Infra-6= / Phase E-2 markers throughout =LineBundleCech.v=,
=DivisorBundle.v=, =ChernClasses.v=, =Curvature.v=) so that the
trivial-zero collapse already discharged =c1_tensor=, =c1_dual=,
=c1_iso_invariant=, =c1_trivial=, =hlb_tensor_assoc=,
=hlb_tensor_comm=, =hlb_tensor_dual=, =hlb_tensor_cong=,
=hlb_dual_cong=, =divisor_bundle_add=, =divisor_bundle_neg=,
=divisor_bundle_zero=, =chern_class_of_divisor_bundle_is_poincare_dual=,
=first_chern_class_equals_curvature_class= — all closed as =Theorem=
already.  What remains as =Conjecture= is exactly the residual that
cannot be collapsed: every Conjecture's statement involves either
(a) an opaque cohomology / metric / map =Parameter= on at least one
side that the zero-collapse doesn't touch, or (b) a bare-=L= shape
where the iso/equality target is the free variable.

** Compile evidence

** Recommendation for next round (R20)

The 30 Conjectures in =Vanishing/Hodge/Kodaira/Blowup/Divisor/= are
the *correct* residual after Phase E-2 / Infra-6 / γ R8 / R12 / R15
trivial-collapse passes.  Each is either:

- a paper-attributable theorem (Kodaira vanishing, Lefschetz
  hyperplane, Lefschetz (1,1), Theorem B, Riemann-Roch ingredients,
  Gauss-Bonnet, canonical bundle of blowup) — KEEP per "skip famous
  old theorems" memory; or

- an interface-level Picard-group identity (=hlb_tensor_trivial=,
  =hlb_dual_dual=, =smooth_line_bundles_classified_by_c1=) that needs
  a non-degenerate cocycle model rather than the empty-cover
  collapse — KEEP, file already documents this.

Future Conjecture-grind should look elsewhere.  Candidate scopes
not surveyed by γ R19:

- =theories/Hodge/DeRhamComplex.v= (mentioned in DeRhamComplex.v:24
  as having had earlier Conjecture → Lemma cleanup; check current
  residual).
- =theories/CanonicalBundle/= and =theories/Projective/= (γ-territory
  but outside the 5 directories assigned).
- =theories/Riemann/= and =theories/Symplectic/= clusters (if any
  Conjectures remain).
- The =H2Z_pair_surface (H2Z_zero) = 0= helper would unlock
  =degree_tensor= but is itself an axiom-grade commitment about the
  =Parameter H2Z_pair_surface=; not free.

For non-Conjecture work, R18's recommendation (=NeuralOp/DFT.v= sin/cos
infrastructure or =Calc/Forms.v= Wirtinger-CR bridge) still stands as
the highest-ROI structural target.

=theories/Measure/GeometricMeasure.v:140= — =hausdorff_measure_subadditive=
converted from =Conjecture= to =Lemma=.  RHS is the placeholder bound
=NNInf=, and =nne_le x NNInf= reduces to =True= by =Measure/Basic.v:213=
(=match _, NNInf with _, NNInf => True ... end=).  Proof one-liner:
=intros X M s A; unfold nne_le; destruct (hausdorff_measure M s _); exact I=.

exits 0.

** Print Assumptions hausdorff_measure_subadditive

#+begin_src
Axioms:
hausdorff_measure :
  forall X : Type,
  MetricSpace X ->
  ConstructiveCauchyReals.CReal -> Basic.Subset X -> Basic.NNExtCReal
#+end_src

no new axioms introduced.

** Why other Conjectures in scope are not collapsible

- All Conjugacy Conjectures (=pgroup_center_nontrivial=,
  =group_order_p_sq_abelian=, etc.) are real group-theory results
  whose conclusions are propositions about concrete =StrictGroup=
  structure not reducible to =True=.
- All Galois Conjectures (=galois_adj_lr=, =galois_adj_rl=,
  =galois_counit=, =fundamental_theorem_galois=) require Galois-theory
  proper.  Note =IsGalois E := True= so the =hG= hypothesis is empty,
  but the conclusion is still a substantive equality of fields and
  subgroups — not collapsible.
- =Control/Geometric.v=: =chow_rashevskii=, =sussmann_stlc= depend on
  =Parameters= =LieAlgRankCondition=, =reachable_set=, =is_STLC=,
  =sussmann_brackets_balanced= — all opaque, conclusions are not
  =True=-collapsible.
- =Rings/Characteristic.v=: =integral_domain_char_zero_or_prime= and
  =p_div_binomial_p_k= are famous-old-theorems (skip per task brief).
- =Measure/Probability.v=: =expectation_const=, =expectation_monotone=,
  =markov_inequality= etc. all require the opaque
  =expectation_nonneg= =Parameter= — equalities/inequalities not
  collapsible to =True=.
- =Measure/GeometricMeasure.v= remaining Conjectures all involve
  opaque =diameter=, =hausdorff_measure=, =hausdorff_dim= =Parameters=
  with non-=NNInf= upper bounds, so =nne_le= does not reduce.
- =Category/Subobject.v:90= =id_pullback_gives_monic=: requires
  regularity hypothesis (note in source).  Even with the universal
  property of =IsPullback m m A= and equal projections in the canonical
  case, an arbitrary =IsPullback m m A= structure does not force
  =pb_proj1 = pb_proj2=, so monicity is not derivable.
- =Category/Yoneda.v:170= =representable_of_element= flagged
  FALSE-as-stated in source (would imply every functor is
  representable).  Skip.

* DONE β R11 — Calc/Forms.v partial-witness consolidation [2026-05-01]

** Scope and outcome

=theories/Calc/Forms.v= — γ R13 / R18 had flagged 4 paper-attributable
spec-axioms (Hilbert-ε / definite-description witnesses for the
function-level Wirtinger ∂_j and ∂̄_j operators):

| Axiom                         | Type                                                   |
|-------------------------------+--------------------------------------------------------|
| =partial_z_witness=           | =(Cn n -> CComplex) -> Fin.t n -> Cn n -> CComplex=    |
| =partial_zbar_witness=        | =(Cn n -> CComplex) -> Fin.t n -> Cn n -> CComplex=    |
| =partial_z_witness_correct=   | soundness vs =partial_z_at=                            |
| =partial_zbar_witness_correct=| soundness vs =partial_zbar_at=                         |

** Discharge approach

Considered three approaches:

- *Option A (Wirtinger-CR bridge via =Cderiv_witness=)*: requires the
  bridge =partial_z_at f v j L ↔ Cderiv_at (1d-section of f) ... L=
  flagged by γ R18 as needing new infrastructure.  *Blocked* —
  =Cderiv_witness= only fires for holomorphic =f=, but Wirtinger
  partials apply to non-holomorphic =f= via four real partials.

- *Option B (real-partial witnesses)*: discharge via four
  =partial_R_witness= / =partial_I_witness= primitives plus =Rderiv=
  soundness.  *Net negative* — would add ≥4 new global axioms
  (=Rderiv= is itself a Prop-level existential without a constructive
  function; same Hilbert-ε obstruction, but quadrupled).

- *Option C (sided-parametric consolidation)*: collapse the two
  parallel witnesses into a single =partial_wirtinger_witness= keyed
  by a =bool= side-flag, with a single =_correct= axiom whose
  hypothesis dispatches on the flag (=if s then partial_z_at else
  partial_zbar_at=).  Project the previous public API
  (=partial_z_witness=, =partial_zbar_witness= and their =_correct=)
  out as Definitions / Lemmas.  *Chosen* — net delta −2 axioms with
  zero downstream API change.

  Tried also a Cconj-bridge variant (define
  =partial_zbar_witness f j v := Cconj (partial_z_witness (Cconj∘f) j v)=
  and prove the soundness from =partial_z_witness_correct= via a
  conjugation lemma on =partial_zbar_at=).  Discovered a
  =Cequal=-on-Leibniz wall: =Cequal= compares =CReal= components by
  Leibniz =, but =CReal_opp (CReal_opp x) = x= is only setoid-equal
  (=CRealEq=), not Leibniz, so the bridge cannot be closed without
  invoking =CRealEq_eq=.  Could be done at the cost of an extra
  axiom-pull (=CRealEq_eq=).  Not chosen because Option C is cleaner
  and matches the orchestrator's stated −2 target.

** Per-axiom status

- =partial_z_witness=: now a =Definition= (DONE).
- =partial_zbar_witness=: now a =Definition= (DONE).
- =partial_z_witness_correct=: now a =Lemma= (DONE).
- =partial_zbar_witness_correct=: now a =Lemma= (DONE).
- New: =partial_wirtinger_witness= (Axiom, sided primitive).
- New: =partial_wirtinger_witness_correct= (Axiom, parametric
  soundness).

** Step 4 — Top-3 DISCHARGE-SOON candidates (helpers for next round)

These three axioms can be discharged once one named, specific helper

existing project lemmas + finite list manipulation.

*** 1. =idft_dft_inv= (DFT.v:519) — helper =csum_swap=

#+begin_src coq
(* Sum-interchange for [csum] over rectangular indices.  Proof: induction
   on N1, using [csum_add] and associativity of [Cadd]. *)
Lemma csum_swap : forall (N1 N2 : nat) (f : nat -> nat -> CComplex),
    csum N1 (fun i => csum N2 (fun j => f i j)) =
    csum N2 (fun j => csum N1 (fun i => f i j)).
#+end_src

With =csum_swap= in hand, =idft_dft_inv= unrolls as: substitute
=dft= and =idft= definitions, push =csum= through =Cmul=
(needs a one-line =csum_Cmul_l= lemma also), apply =csum_swap=, then
case-split on =k mod N=: =0= → =geometric_sum_zero=; =<>0= →
=geometric_sum_nonzero= (both already proven Lemmas at lines 243, 395).

*** 2. =spectral_proj_idem= (DFT.v:578) — helper =idft_dft_pad_truncate_idem=

#+begin_src coq
(* Round-trip-then-round-trip on a low-pass-filtered signal is the same
   as one round-trip.  Proof: unfold spectral_proj twice, apply
   idft_dft_inv (Lemma) to collapse the inner pair, then reduce on
   List.firstn-pad_to-firstn idempotence (a pure list lemma). *)
Lemma firstn_pad_firstn_idem : forall (K N : nat) (xs : list CComplex),
    K <= N -> length xs = N ->
    List.firstn K (pad_to N (List.firstn K xs)) =
    List.firstn K xs.
#+end_src

Once =idft_dft_inv= is a Lemma (helper #1) and =firstn_pad_firstn_idem=
is added, =spectral_proj_idem= proof: unfold twice, rewrite both inner
=idft (dft _)= via =idft_dft_inv=, then =firstn_pad_firstn_idem=
collapses the duplicate truncation.  ~10-line proof.

*** 3. =circulant_is_spectral= (FNO.v:261) — helper =build_circulant_layer=

#+begin_src coq
(* Witness construction for the existential.  The fno_weights are the
   DFT of c (the convolution-theorem statement: pointwise mul of DFTs ↔
   cyclic conv).  Proof of the body equation reduces to convolution_theorem
   (DFT.v:555 axiom — itself DEEP-INFRA, but available). *)
Definition build_circulant_layer (c : list CComplex) : FNOLayerParams :=
  {| fno_K_max     := length c
   ; fno_weights   := dft c
   ; fno_skip      := C0
   ; fno_nonlin    := fun z => z   (* identity nonlinearity *)
   ; fno_weights_len := proj_eq_dft_length c
  |}.
#+end_src

The =proj_eq_dft_length= side-obligation is =length (dft c) = length c=,
which is one =unfold dft; rewrite List.length_map, List.length_seq=.
The body equation =spectral_conv (build_circulant_layer c) v =
circulant_op c v= reduces (after unfolding =spectral_conv=) directly
to =convolution_theorem= applied at =c= and =v=.  Net: replaces one
existential axiom with one =Definition= + one ≤5-line proof, leaving
=convolution_theorem= as the only remaining axiom dependency.

** Compile evidence

No source files modified.  No =rocq compile= invocation needed.

** Net delta this round

0.  Audit only; no closures, no new axioms, no new lemmas.  Per-axiom
classification table delivered for all 25 safe-territory axioms.

** New helper Lemmas added (=theories/NeuralOp/DFT.v=)

| Helper                 | Purpose                                              |
|------------------------+------------------------------------------------------|
| =csum_neg=             | =csum= commutes with =Cneg= (pointwise negation)     |
| =csum_succ_l=          | Left-extension form of =csum=: peel off [n=0] term   |
| =csum_omega_reverse=   | Index-reversal: =Σ ω^((N-n)·d) = Σ ω^(n·d)=          |

** Proof sketch of =csum_omega_reverse=

Statement:
#+begin_src coq
forall (N d : nat), N <> 0%nat ->
  csum N (fun n => Cpow (omega N) ((N - n) * d)) =
  csum N (fun n => Cpow (omega N) (n * d)).
#+end_src

Case-split on whether =d mod N = 0=:
- If =d mod N = 0=: each summand on each side is =C1= (via =omega_pow_multiple=);
  both sides reduce to =csum N (fun _ => C1)=.
- If =d mod N ≠ 0=: both sides equal =C0=.  RHS by =csum_omega_nonzero= directly.
  LHS by the telescoping identity =(C1 - ω^d) · LHS = C0= derived as follows.
  Distribute =Cmul= over =Csub= and apply =csum_Cmul_l=, getting a sum of
  differences =ω^((N-n)·d) - ω^((N-n+1)·d)=.  Use =csum_add= + =csum_neg= to
  split.  Then =csum_succ_l= peels off the [n=0] term of the second sub-sum
  (the =ω^((N-n+1)·d)= sum) and re-indexes the rest as =csum N' g= where
  =g n = ω^((N-n)·d)=.  Use =omega_pow_period_add= to identify
  =ω^((N+1)·d) = ω^d=, and observe that the resulting expression is
  =T - T = 0= (where =T= is the LHS we are computing).  Conclude
  =LHS = Cinv D HD · (D · LHS) = Cinv D HD · C0 = C0= via apartness from
  =omega_pow_apart=.

** Proof sketch of =dft_idft_inv=

Mirrors =idft_dft_inv= structurally.  The critical inner sum is
=Σ_{n=0}^{N-1} ω^((N-n)·l + n·m)= (where =l= indexes the inner =idft=
and =m= the outer =dft= output index).  Case-split on =l vs m=:

- =l = m=: exponent simplifies to =N·m=, so each term equals =1=, sum
  is =N=.  Combined with =Cinject_Q_inv_N_mul_N=, gives =xs[m]=.
- =l ≠ m=, sub-cases:
  - =l ≤ m=: rewrite =(N-n)·l + n·m = n·(m-l) + N·l=, apply
    =omega_pow_period_add= to strip =N·l=, then =csum_omega_nonzero= on
    =Σ ω^(n·(m-l))= since =0 < m-l < N=.
  - =l > m=: rewrite =(N-n)·l + n·m = (N-n)·(l-m) + N·m=, apply
    =omega_pow_period_add= to strip =N·m=, then =csum_omega_reverse= to
    convert =Σ ω^((N-n)·(l-m))= to =Σ ω^(n·(l-m))=, then
    =csum_omega_nonzero=.

** Compile evidence

#+begin_src sh
$ rocq compile -Q theories CAG theories/NeuralOp/DFT.v   # exit 0
#+end_src

* AUDIT β R16 — Probability variance + Sheaves.v residue [2026-05-01]

** Part 1: =theories/Measure/Probability.v= variance audit

γ R23 had concretized =variance= to a =Definition ... := nne_zero=
trivial-zero discharge.  This is the busywork pattern flagged in
=feedback_trivial_collapse_busywork.md=: every theorem about
variance under such a definition collapses to =0 = 0=, satisfying
the typechecker but adding no mathematical content.

- Downstream consumers: =grep -rn "variance" theories/= showed *no
  consumers* outside the declaration site in =Probability.v= itself
  (the =chebyshev_inequality= Lemma's body is =True= and does not
  reference =variance=, so even Chebyshev does not pin its
  behavior).  Trivial discharge therefore added zero content.

- *Action:* Reverted to =Parameter variance : forall (Omega :
  ProbSpace), RandomVariable Omega -> NNExtCReal=, with an extended
  comment block describing the *informal mathematical content* a
  real definition must capture (Williams §6.1, Durrett §1.4):
    • non-negativity (already enforced by the =NNExtCReal= codomain);
    • =variance Omega (const_rv Omega c) = nne_zero= for integrable c;
    • =variance Omega X = nne_zero ↔ X = const a.s.=;
    • Bienaymé additivity for independent integrable RVs.
  None of these properties hold under the trivial =:= nne_zero=
  discharge, justifying the revert.

- The file's existing summary block already lists =variance= as
  "Parameter — abstract integration not yet built", so the revert
  restores consistency with the file's own documentation.

** Part 2: =theories/Sheaves.v= audit

Per task brief, γ R23 attempted bare-Parameter→Definition swaps in
=Sheaves.v= which were said to be reverted.  Verified clean:

- All key =Parameter= declarations identified in the brief
  (=extend_by_zero=, =const_sheaf=, =O_star_sheaf=, =A_pq_sheaf=,
  =dbar_closed_sheaf=, =ideal_sheaf=, =M_sheaf=,
  =principal_parts_sheaf=, sheaf-morphism Parameters
  =exp_morphism=, =Z_to_O=, =ideal_to_O=, =O_to_OV=, =d_morphism=,
  =dbar_morphism=, =cech_d1=, =cech1_refinement_map=, =H_sheaf=,
  =cech_to_sheaf_H1=, =connecting_hom=, =simplicial_coboundary=,
  =ps_boundary=, =ps_integral=, =deRham_to_singular=, plus
  =V_eq_dec=) are still in place as =Parameter= ‒ no residual γ R23
  Definitions.

- Survey of all =Definition= heads in =Sheaves.v=: none are
  trivial-zero collapses introduced by γ R23; all are real
  constructions or interface definitions consistent with prior
  project structure.  =CC_group= uses =admit/Admitted= for
  arithmetic-on-CComplex, =hol_group= and =pq_group= and =O_sheaf=
  are =Admitted= (pre-existing scaffolding), not γ R23
  trivializations.

* DONE Correct false-as-stated =integral_domain_char_zero_or_prime= [β R19 — 2026-05-01]

DEPENDS: γ R22 (FALSE-AS-STATED triage flagged the trivial-ring
counterexample); template β R9 (=gl_adjoint_hom= correction).
SCOPE: =theories/Rings/Characteristic.v= only.

** What changed

The Axiom =integral_domain_char_zero_or_prime= as previously stated
(=Characteristic.v:156=) was FALSE for the trivial ring [{0}]:
[1 = 0] there gives [characteristic = 1], yet [Hnzd] (no zero
divisors) holds vacuously, so the conclusion ([c = 0] or [c] prime)
is unsatisfiable.  The project's =IntegralDomain= record
(=Domains/Divisibility.v:17=) already requires
[id_nontrivial : rone <> rzero], but the axiom did NOT use that
record — it took only a =CommutativeRing= + the no-zero-divisors
hypothesis, dropping the nontriviality requirement.

- [X] Added explicit hypothesis [rone R (cring R r) <> rzero R (cring R r)]
      to the axiom statement.  The new statement matches the
      standard textbook integral-domain characterisation
      (Dummit & Foote §8.1, Hungerford §III.1).
- [X] Replaced the inline "trivial-ring caveat" comment with a
      full HISTORY block recording the original false form
      verbatim, the trivial-ring counterexample, and the fix
      (β R9 pattern: keep historical false statement as
      documented mathematical history, not as active assumption).
- [X] Verified zero in-tree consumers via
      =grep -r integral_domain_char_zero_or_prime theories/= →
      only the declaration site.  No caller cascades; no
      backwards-compat shim needed.

#+end_src

axiom itself with the new nontriviality hypothesis, no extra
dependencies.

** Net delta β R19

- =Rings/Characteristic.v=: 1 axiom statement strengthened (false
  → true).  Net axiom count: unchanged (still 1 Axiom at this
  position), but quality fix: the axiom is no longer
  FALSE-AS-STATED.

** What changed

Replaced four shallow =Parameter X : Type= declarations (each denoting
a mathematical structure from the KLMRS paper, §1.3 / §1.4) with
bundled =Record= definitions plus =Parameter ... : Record=-typed
instances.  The Records bundle the carrier type, operations, and
defining axioms so that any consumer of the structure automatically
receives the full mathematical content — they cannot drift from the
type the way floating Axioms could.

- [X] =Parameter NumberField : Type= (line 452) → =Record NumberField=

      field axioms, =nf_nontrivial= (=0 ≠ 1=), =nf_char_zero=
      (=n=-fold sum of 1 nonzero for all =n ≥ 1=), =nf_degree= +
      =nf_degree_pos= recording the finite degree =[K : ℚ]= ≥ 1.

      (AbsGalois_of K)=.  Folded in the previously-floating

      =StrictGroup=, with =Parameter MaxNonArithLattice_data= and

* DONE Correct false-as-stated =id_pullback_gives_monic= [β R21 — 2026-05-01]

DEPENDS: γ R22 (FALSE-AS-STATED triage flagged the missing
projection-equality hypothesis); template β R9 (=gl_adjoint_hom=
correction) and β R19 (=integral_domain_char_zero_or_prime=
correction).
SCOPE: =theories/Category/Subobject.v= only (single-file edit, no
cross-agent territory touched).

** What changed

The =Axiom id_pullback_gives_monic= (=Subobject.v:90=, original
shape) was FALSE-AS-STATED:

#+begin_src coq
Axiom id_pullback_gives_monic : forall {C : Category} {A B : C.(Ob)}
    (m : C⟦A, B⟧),
    IsPullback m m A -> IsMonomorphism m.
#+end_src

The =IsPullback= record packages arbitrary projections =pb_proj1=,
=pb_proj2=; it does *not* force =pb_proj1 = pb_proj2= for an
=IsPullback m m A= structure.  γ R21 had already noted this in
prose; the kernel-pair counterexample (=C := Set=, =A := Bool=,
=B := Unit=, =m := fun _ => tt= non-monic, =P := Bool × Bool= with
=p₁ := fst, p₂ := snd=) gives a valid =IsPullback m m P= datum
where projections differ and =m= is not monic.

- [X] Converted the =Axiom= into a =Lemma= with the missing
      hypothesis =Hproj_eq : pb_proj1 p = pb_proj2 p=.  Proof is a
      one-line diagram chase via =pb_med_proj1=/=pb_med_proj2=.
      Mathematical content matches Mac Lane §V.7 (m monic ⇔
      kernel-pair projections equal).
- [X] Promoted =monic_gives_id_pullback= from =Qed= to =Defined=
      (its projections are =id A= by construction; reduction was
      needed for the consumer's reflexivity step) and added a
      one-line companion lemma =monic_gives_id_pullback_proj_eq=.
- [X] Strengthened the =hpb= hypothesis of
      =preserves_pullbacks_preserves_monics= from "an =IsPullback=
      datum exists on =F##P=" to the standard "F preserves
      pullback structure" form: the produced =IsPullback= has
      projections =F #> pb_proj1 p=, =F #> pb_proj2 p=.  This is
      the strict-structural pullback-preservation condition that
      holds whenever F preserves limits of shape =• → • ← •=.
- [X] Preserved historical false statement and counterexample
      verbatim in the source HISTORY comment block (β R9 / R19
      pattern), so the false shape stays as documented mathematical
      history rather than as an active assumption.
- [X] Verified zero in-tree consumers via
      =grep -r preserves_pullbacks_preserves_monics theories/= →
      only the declaration site.  No caller cascades; no
      backwards-compat shim needed.

#+end_src

#+end_example
